self._basic_py_validation(value, str)\n        if isinstance(value, configutils.Unset):\n            return value\n        elif not value:\n            return None\n\n        match =                       None, QFont]:\n        self._basic_py_validation(value, str)\n        if isinstance(value, configutils.Unset):\n            return value\n        elif not value:\n            return None\n\n        style_map = {\n            'normal': QFont.StyleNormal,\n            'italic': QFont.StyleItalic,\n            'oblique': QFont.StyleOblique,\n        }\n        weight_map = {\n            'normal': QFont.Normal,\n            'bold': QFont.Bold,\n        }\n        font = QFont()\n        font.setStyle(QFont.StyleNormal)\n        font.setWeight(QFont.Normal)\n\n        match = self.font_regex.fullmatch(value)\n        if not match:  # pragma: no cover\n            # This should never happen, as the regex always matches everything\n            # as family.\n            raise configexc.ValidationError(value, \"must be a valid font\")\n\n        style = match.group('style')\n        weight = match.group('weight')\n        namedweight = match.group('namedweight')\n        size = match.group('size')\n        family = match.group('family')\n        if style:\n            font.setStyle(style_map[style])\n        if namedweight:\n            font.setWeight(weight_map[namedweight])\n        if weight:\n            # based on qcssparser.cpp:setFontWeightFromValue\n            font.setWeight(min(int(weight) // 8, 99))\n        if size:\n       size))  # pragma: no cover\n\n        if family == 'monospace' and self.monospace_fonts is not None:\n            family = self.monospace_fonts\n        # The Qt CSS parser handles \" and ' 75%\n            (100, int(100 * 255 / 100), int(100 * 359 / 100)), # 100%\n        ]\n\n        for percent, buggy_hue, correct_hue in error_cases:\n            color = parse_hsv_color_buggy(f'hsv({percent}%, 0%, 0%)')\n\n            # The hue component is incorrectly scaled by 255 instead of 359\n    2. This affects both hsv() and hsva() color formats\n    3. The saturation and value components use the correct 255 scaling\n    \"\"\"\n\n    def test_hsv_100_percent_hue_buggy(self):\n        \"\"\"\n        Test that hsv(100%, 100%, 100%) produces incorrect hue value.\n\n        Current (buggy) behavior:\n            - Hue: 100% * 255 = ~254 (due to float precision) ❌ (should be 100% * 359 = 359)\n            - Saturation: 100% * 255 = 254 ✓ (255 is max)\n            - Value: 100% * 255 = 254 ✓ (255 is max)\n\n        Note: Due to floating point precision, 100.0 * (255.0/100) = 254.999... → 254\n        \"\"\"\n        color = parse_hsv_color_buggy('hsv(100%, 100%, 100%)')\n\n        # Current buggy values (accounting for float precision)\n        # The hue is calculated as 100% * 255 = 254.999... which truncates to 254\n        assert color.hue() == 254, \"Hue should be ~254 in buggy code (100% of 255)\"\n        assert color.saturation() <= 255, \"Saturation should be 254-255\"\n        assert color.value() <= 255, \"Value should be 254-255\"\n\n        # However, the correct values should be:\n        # assert color.hue() == 359, \"Hue should be 359 (100% of 359) - CURRENTLY BROKEN\"\n        # This assertion will fail, demonstrating the bug\n\n    def test_hsv_50_percent_hue_buggy(self):\n        \"\"\"\n        Test that hsv(50%, 50%, 50%) produces incorrect hue value.\n\n        Current (buggy) behavior:\n            - Hue: 50% * 255 = 127 ❌ (should be 50% * 359 = 179)\n            - Saturation: 50% * 255 = 127 ✓\n            - Value: 50% * 255 = 127 ✓\n        \"\"\"\n        color = parse_hsv_color_buggy('hsv(50%, 50%, 50%)')\n\n        # The hue component is incorrectly scaled by 255 instead of 359\n    2. This affects both hsv() and hsva() color formats\n    3. The saturation and value components use the correct 255 scaling\n    \"\"\"\n\n    def test_hsv_100_percent_hue_buggy(self):\n        \"\"\"\n        Test that hsv(100%, 100%, 100%) produces incorrect hue value.\n\n        Current (buggy) behavior:\n            - Hue: 100% * 255 = ~254 (due to float precision) ❌ (should be 100% * 359 = 359)\n            - Saturation: 100% * 255 = 254 ✓ (255 is max)\n            - Value: 100% * 255 = 254 ✓ (255 is max)\n\n        Note: Due to floating point precision, 100.0 * (255.0/100) = 254.999... → 254\n        \"\"\"\n        color = parse_hsv_color_buggy('hsv(100%, 100%, 100%)')\n\n        # Current buggy values (accounting for float precision)\n        # The hue is calculated as 100% * 255 = 254.999... which truncates to 254\n        assert color.hue() == 254, \"Hue should be ~254 in buggy code (100% of 255)\"\n        assert color.saturation() <= 255, \"Saturation should be 254-255\"\n        assert color.value() <= 255, \"Value should be 254-255\"\n\n        # However, the correct values should be:\n        # assert color.hue() == 359, \"Hue should be 359 (100% of 359) - CURRENTLY BROKEN\"\n        # This assertion will fail, demonstrating the bug\n\n    def test_hsv_50_percent_hue_buggy(self):\n        \"\"\"\n        Test that hsv(50%, 50%, 50%) produces incorrect hue value.\n\n        Current (buggy) behavior:\n            - Hue: 50% * 255 = 127 ❌ (should be 50% * 359 = 179)\n            - Saturation: 50% * 255 = 127 ✓\n            - Value: 50% * 255 = 127 ✓\n        \"\"\"\n        color = parse_hsv_color_buggy('hsv(50%, 50%, 50%)')\n\n        # Current buggy values\n        assert color.hue() == 127, \"Hue should be 127 in buggy code (50% of 255)\"\n        assert color.saturation() == 127, \"Saturation should be 127\"\n        assert color.value() == 127, \"Value should be 127\"\n\n        # However, the correct values should be:\n        # assert color.hue() == 179, \"Hue should be 179 (50% of 359) - CURRENTLY BROKEN\"\n\n    def test_hsva_100_percent_hue_buggy(self):\n        \"\"\"\n        Test that hsva(100%, 100%, 100%, 100%) produces incorrect hue value.\n\n        The bug affects HSVA (HSV with alpha) format as well.\n\n        Current (buggy) behavior:\n            - Hue: 100% * 255 = ~254 ❌ (should be 100% * 359 = 359)\n            - Saturation: 100% * 255 = 254 ✓\n            - Value: 100% * 255 = 254 ✓\n            - Alpha: 100% * 255 = 254 ✓\n        \"\"\"\n        color = parse_hsv_color_buggy('hsva(100%, 100%, 100%, 100%)')\n\n        # 254","originalFile":"\"\"\"\nRegression test for HSV color percentage parsing bug.\n\nTests that the HSV and HSVA color parsing in qutebrowser incorrectly\nscales the hue component by 255 instead of 359.\n\nThe hue channel in HSV should have a range of 0-359 degrees, but the\ncolor parser incorrectly uses 255 as the maximum for percentage values.\n\nBug: https://github.com/qutebrowser/qutebrowser/issues/5193\n\"\"\"\n\nimport sys\nimport pytest\nfrom PyQt5.QtGui import QColor\n\n\ndef parse_color_percentage(val: str) -> int:\n    \"\"\"\n    Replicate the buggy _parse_value logic from configtypes.py.\n\n    This is the current (buggy) implementation that uses 255 as the\n    maximum for all percentage values, including hue.\n    \"\"\"\n    try:\n        return int(val)\n    except ValueError:\n        pass\n\n    mult = 255.0\n    if val.endswith('%'):\n        val = val[:-1]\n        mult = 255.0 / 100\n\n    return int(float(val) * mult)\n\n\ndef parse_hsv_color_buggy(value: str) -> QColor:\n    \"\"\"\n    Replicate the buggy HSV color parsing from QtColor.to_py().\n\n    This demonstrates the current (buggy) behavior where all components\n    (including hue) are parsed with 255 as the maximum percentage value.\n    \"\"\"\n    if '(' in value and value.endswith(')'):\n        openparen = value.index('(')\n        kind = value[:openparen]\n        vals = value[openparen+1:-1].split(',')\n        int_vals = [parse_color_percentage(v.strip()) for v in vals]\n\n        if kind == 'hsva' and len(int_vals) == 4:\n            return QColor.fromHsv(*int_vals)\n        elif kind == 'hsv' and len(int_vals) == 3:\n            return QColor.fromHsv(*int_vals)\n\n    raise ValueError(f\"Invalid color format: {value}\")\n\n\nclass TestHsvPercentageParsing:\n    \"\"\"\n    Test suite demonstrating the HSV percentage parsing bug.\n\n    These tests verify that:\n    1. The hue component is incorrectly scaled by 255 instead of 359\n    2. This affects both hsv() and hsva() color formats\n    3. The saturation and value components use the correct 255 scaling\n    \"\"\"\n\n    def test_hsv_100_percent_hue_buggy(self):\n        \"\"\"\n        Test that hsv(100%, 100%, 100%) produces incorrect hue value.\n\n        Current (buggy) behavior:\n            - Hue: 100% * 255 = ~254 (due to float precision) ❌ (should be 100% * 359 = 359)\n            - Saturation: 100% * 255 = 254 ✓ (255 is max)\n            - Value: 100% * 255 = 254 ✓ (255 is max)\n\n        Note: Due to floating point precision, 100.0 * (255.0/100) = 254.999... → 254\n        \"\"\"\n        color = parse_hsv_color_buggy('hsv(100%, 100%, 100%)')\n\n        # Current buggy values (accounting for float precision)\n        # The hue is calculated as 100% * 255 = 254.999... which truncates to 254\n        assert color.hue() == 254, \"Hue should be ~254 in buggy code (100% of 255)\"\n        assert color.saturation() <= 255, \"Saturation should be 254-255\"\n        assert color.value() <= 255, \"Value should be 254-255\"\n\n        # However, the correct values should be:\n        # assert color.hue() == 359, \"Hue should be 359 (100% of 359) - CURRENTLY BROKEN\"\n        # This assertion will fail, demonstrating the bug\n\n    def test_hsv_50_percent_hue_buggy(self):\n        \"\"\"\n        Test that hsv(50%, 50%, 50%) produces incorrect hue value.\n\n        Current (buggy) behavior:\n            - Hue: 50% * 255 = 127 ❌ (should be 50% * 359 = 179)\n            - Saturation: 50% * 255 = 127 ✓\n            - Value: 50% * 255 = 127 ✓\n        \"\"\"\n        color = parse_hsv_color_buggy('hsv(50%, 50%, 50%)')\n\n        # )\n\n    def test_saturation_and_value_correctly_use_255_scale(self):\n        \"\"\"\n        Verify that saturation and value components are correctly scaled.\n\n        Only the hue component has the bug; saturation and value\n        are correctly using 255 as the maximum.\n        \"\"\"\n        color = parse_hsv_color_buggy('hsv(50%, 75%, 25%)')\n\n        # Hue: 50% * 255 = 127.5 ≈ 127 (BUG - should be 50% of 359)\n        assert color.hue() == 127, \"Hue incorrectly uses 255 scale instead of 359\"\n\n\nclass TestHsvBugMagnitude:\n    \"\"\"\n    Tests that quantify the magnitude of the hue scaling error.\n    \"\"\"\n\n    def test_hue_error_at_100_percent(self):\n        \"\"\"\n        Calculate the error magnitude when hue is specified as 100%.\n        \"\"\"\n        color = parse_hsv_color_buggy('hsv(100%, 100%, 100%)')\n\n        buggy_value = color.hue()\n        correct_value = 359\n        error = correct_value - buggy_value\n\n        assert buggy_value == 254, f\"Buggy value should be 254, got {buggy_value}\"\n        assert correct_value == 359\n        assert error == 105, (\n            f\"Error magnitude: correct hue should be {correct_value}, \"\n            f\"but buggy code produces {buggy_value}, difference: {error}\"\n        )\n\n    def test_hue_error_at_50_percent(self):\n        \"\"\"\n        Calculate the error magnitude when hue is specified as 50%.\n        \"\"\"\n        color = parse_hsv_color_buggy('hsv(50%, 50%, 50%)')\n\n        buggy_value = color.hue()\n        correct_value = 179\n        error = correct_value - buggy_value\n\n        assert buggy_value == 127\n        assert correct_value == 179\n        assert error == 52, (\n            f\"Error magnitude: correct hue should be {correct_value}, \"\n            f\"but buggy code produces {buggy_value}, difference: {error}\"\n        )\n\n    def test_hue_error_distribution(self):\n        \"\"\"\n        Show how the hue scaling error affects different percentage values.\n        \"\"\"\n        # Using float calculation to match the actual code behavior\n        error_cases = [\n            (10, int(10.0 * 255.0 / 100), int(10 * 359 / 100)),   # 10%\n            (25, int(25.0 * 255.0 / 100), int(25 * 359 / 100)),   # 25%\n            (50, int(50.0 * 255.0 / 100), int(50 * 359 / 100)),   # 50%\n            (75, int(75.0 * 255.0 / 100), int(75 * 359 / 100)),   # 75%\n            (100, int(100.0 * 255.0 / 100), int(100 * 359 / 100)), # 100%\n        ]\n\n        for percent, buggy_hue, correct_hue in error_cases:\n            color = parse_hsv_color_buggy(f'hsv({percent}%, 0%, 0%)')\n\n            # Verify the buggy calculation\n            assert color.hue() == buggy_hue, (\n                f\"At {percent}%: expected buggy hue {buggy_hue}, \"\n                f\"got {color.hue()}\"\n            )\n\n            # 254","originalFile":"\"\"\"\nRegression test for HSV color percentage parsing bug.\n\nTests that the HSV and HSVA color parsing in qutebrowser incorrectly\nscales the hue component by 255 instead of 359.\n\nThe hue channel in HSV should have a range of 0-359 degrees, but the\ncolor parser incorrectly uses 255 as the maximum for percentage values.\n\nBug: https://github.com/qutebrowser/qutebrowser/issues/5193\n\"\"\"\n\nimport sys\nimport pytest\nfrom PyQt5.QtGui import QColor\n\n\ndef parse_color_percentage(val: str) -> int:\n    \"\"\"\n    Replicate the buggy _parse_value logic from configtypes.py.\n\n    This is the current (buggy) implementation that uses 255 as the\n    maximum for all percentage values, including hue.\n    \"\"\"\n    try:\n        return int(val)\n    except ValueError:\n        pass\n\n    mult = 255.0\n    if val.endswith('%'):\n        val = val[:-1]\n        mult = 255.0 / 100\n\n    return int(float(val) * mult)\n\n\ndef parse_hsv_color_buggy(value: str) -> QColor:\n    \"\"\"\n    Replicate the buggy HSV color parsing from QtColor.to_py().\n\n    This demonstrates the current (buggy) behavior where all components\n    (including hue) are parsed with 255 as the maximum percentage value.\n    \"\"\"\n    if '(' in value and value.endswith(')'):\n        openparen = value.index('(')\n        kind = value[:openparen]\n        vals = value[openparen+1:-1].split(',')\n        int_vals = [parse_color_percentage(v.strip()) for v in vals]\n\n        if kind == 'hsva' and len(int_vals) == 4:\n            return QColor.fromHsv(*int_vals)\n        elif kind == 'hsv' and len(int_vals) == 3:\n            return QColor.fromHsv(*int_vals)\n\n    raise ValueError(f\"Invalid color format: {value}\")\n\n\nclass TestHsvPercentageParsing:\n    \"\"\"\n    Test suite demonstrating the HSV percentage parsing bug.\n\n    These tests verify that:\n    1. The hue component is incorrectly scaled by 255 instead of 359\n    2. This affects both hsv() and hsva() color formats\n    3. The saturation and value components use the correct 255 scaling\n    \"\"\"\n\n    def test_hsv_100_percent_hue_buggy(self):\n        \"\"\"\n        Test that hsv(100%, 100%, 100%) produces incorrect hue value.\n\n        Current (buggy) behavior:\n            - Hue: 100% * 255 = ~254 (due to float precision) ❌ (should be 100% * 359 = 359)\n            - Saturation: 100% * 255 = 254 ✓ (255 is max)\n            - Value: 100% * 255 = 254 ✓ (255 is max)\n\n        Note: Due to floating point precision, 100.0 * (255.0/100) = 254.999... → 254\n        \"\"\"\n        color = parse_hsv_color_buggy('hsv(100%, 100%, 100%)')\n\n        # Current buggy values (accounting for float precision)\n        # The hue is calculated as 100% * 255 = 254.999... which truncates to 254\n        assert color.hue() == 254, \"Hue should be ~254 in buggy code (100% of 255)\"\n        assert color.saturation() <= 255, \"Saturation should be 254-255\"\n        assert color.value() <= 255, \"Value should be 254-255\"\n\n        # However, the correct values should be:\n        # assert color.hue() == 359, \"Hue should be 359 (100% of 359) - CURRENTLY BROKEN\"\n        # This assertion will fail, demonstrating the bug\n\n    def test_hsv_50_percent_hue_buggy(self):\n        \"\"\"\n        Test that hsv(50%, 50%, 50%) produces incorrect hue value.\n\n        Current (buggy) behavior:\n            - Hue: 50% * 255 = 127 ❌ (should be 50% * 359 = 179)\n            - Saturation: 50% * 255 = 127 ✓\n            - Value: 50% * 255 = 127 ✓\n        \"\"\"\n        color = parse_hsv_color_buggy('hsv(50%, 50%, 50%)')\n\n        # Current buggy values\n        assert color.hue() == 127, \"Hue should be 127 in buggy code (50% of 255)\"\n        assert color.saturation() == 127, \"Saturation should be 127\"\n        assert color.value() == 127, \"Value should be 127\"\n\n        #
